\n</h1>\n\n<br class=\"clear\">\n\n\n        <!-- START ARTICLE POSITION 1 -->\n        \n                <div class=\"ipsBox\">\n                        <div class=\"ipsBox_container ipsPad\">\n                                \n                                <div id=\"jkhsub\"><h2 class=\"ipsType_subtitle\">\n                                        \n\n                                        \n                                        \n                                        \n                                        <a href=\"https://jkhub.org/page/index.html/_/interviews/mod-feature-epic-challenge-mod-iii-r136\">Mod Feature: Epic Challenge Mod III</a>\n                                </h2></div>\n                                <div class=\"desc\">Apr 12 2017 07:29 PM | <a hovercard-ref=\"member\" hovercard-id=\"122\" data-ipb=\"noparse\" class=\"url fn name  ___hover___member _hoversetup\" href=\"https://jkhub.org/user/122-circa/\" title=\"\" id=\"anonymous_element_1\"><span itemprop=\"name\">Circa</span></a> in <a href=\"https://jkhub.org/page/index.html/_/interviews/\">Interviews</a></div>\n                                <br>\n                                <p><!-- isHtml:1 --><!-- isHtml:1 --></p><p style=\"text-align:center\"><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" alt=\"yRmMD1c.png\" src=\"http://i.imgur.com/yRmMD1c.png\"></span></p><p style=\"text-align:center\"><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" alt=\"WiU3kuo.jpg\" src=\"http://i.imgur.com/WiU3kuo.jpg\"></span></p><br>\n<p>Hello friends. It’s been awhile since writing a legit article around here. I want to do more, but both lack of motivation and topics makes it difficult. I think this may change from now on, because we are starting a new article series, called Mod Features!<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\nMod Features will be exactly what it sounds like: an article dedicated to showing off a mod, what it features, small interviews with the creators, etc.<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\nThe first mod to get this special treatment is the Epic Challenge Mod III. Now, apparently this mod has been in development for a few years, with a couple previous versions made. If you were like me and had no idea this mod project even existed until recently, you should definitely check it out.<br>\n&nbsp;</p><br>\n<span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"http://i.imgur.com/Am9OICy.jpg\" align=\"left\" hspace=\"10\" vspace=\"10\" width=\"350\" height=\"auto\"></span><p><span style=\"font-size:24px\">A little about the mod</span><br>\nEpic Challenge Mod III is a single player mod, complete with it’s own story, maps, enemies, and quirky thematic choices that make you feel like you’re in a Star Wars-themed Nintendo game. The amount of content in this mod is vastly great, arguably more than even the base Jedi Academy single player story. This mod took the creator, RJA, almost 2 years, which definitely shows in the amount of stuff there is in this thing. You will find yourself fighting to survive enemies that are in your way of an objective, or you may just need to find a way to reach a certain area of the map in a certain way. Much of this mod will involve using your brain and survival skills to reach the end.</p><br>\n<p>The story features a villain named Darth Lawn, which has created this “Zone of Trouble” to which you play as Kyle and a couple new characters, with help from Luke, to defeat him. Each area you reach contains various challenges ranging from a great number of NPCs, or a few tough NPCs, or certain climbing and jumping obstacles, and much more. Many areas are complex to where you need to get one area unlocked or retrieve something, and make the trek back to where you started to find a new unlocked door or pathway. The effort put into creating all that is admirable. You don’t see that in many JKA mods like this.</p>&nbsp;<br>\n<span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"http://i.imgur.com/UIgCq6P.jpg\" align=\"right\" hspace=\"10\" vspace=\"10\" width=\"350\" height=\"auto\"></span><p>One of the first things you’ll notice is the charming French accent. RJA voiced most of the characters in the mod. As an English-speaker, hearing Kyle and Luke with a French accent speaking English was very amusing, especially since it was the same person with a different inflection. The <img src=\"https://jkhub.org/public/style_emoticons/default/tongue.png\" class=\"bbc_emoticon\" alt=\":P\">&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;</p><p>&nbsp;<br>\nOverall, the mod can be very difficult, especially for new players. Saving often is my best advice. I think my biggest challenge was getting used to the single player movement, after playing multiplayer for so long. The movement is very different in each. So climbing up a bunch of platforms to reach the top of a mountain was a great challenge for me, whereas it would have been cake if it was multiplayer. <img src=\"https://jkhub.org/public/style_emoticons/default/tongue.png\" class=\"bbc_emoticon\" alt=\":P\"> The NPCs can be difficult as well. Sometimes you have to favor sneaking around huge hordes of them instead of attempting to fight them all at once.<br>\n&nbsp;</p><p>&nbsp;<br>\n<span style=\"font-size:24px\">A short interview</span><br>\nI took a bit of time asking the creator of Epic Challenge Mod III, RJA, a few questions about his mod, to get some more info about his process, inspiration, and more.<br>\n</p><p><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"https://i.imgur.com/SQ04n1o.png\"></span><br>\n<em><strong>So what gave you the idea to make a mod like this? Was there anything outside of Jedi Academy that inspired your work?</strong></em><br>\n<em><strong><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"http://i.imgur.com/cCHzEnE.png\" style=\"float: right;\"></span></strong></em><br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\nI would say the real goal is to propose challenges to everyone, but I'm with those who think that every creator has a personnal purpose. Mine was an obsession to revisit the games I played in my childhood, especially early childhood. It was some kind of porting impressions, sensations in my favourite game (which is Jedi Academy).<br>\nSo what inspired me where these games. This mod is the third one I made for SP. Like the others, some parts of are based from a game I used to played in the early last decade. If ECMI was inspired by Croc: Legend Of The Gobbos and ECMII: Rayman 2: The Great Escape, this one took a lot from Tonic Trouble, an underrated UbiSoft game made the year before Rayman 2 (it was supposed to test 3d Games rayman-lookalike before releasing the true Rayman 2). Tonic Trouble gave me the taste of absurdity, psychedelism.<br>\nThe form of the mod came in a simple way. I always knew It would be my thing to make HUGE MODS (like 35-55 maps), with a lot of ennemies, places, challenges and the best of all... secrets. This one has a <em>lot</em> of secrets. And my passion about secrets came from these platform games I used to play.<br>\n<span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"https://i.imgur.com/SQ04n1o.png\"></span><br>\n<em><strong>How long did it take to complete Epic Challenge Mod III? How does that compare to the previous versions of the mod?</strong></em><br>\n<em><strong><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"http://i.imgur.com/cCHzEnE.png\" style=\"float: right;\"></span></strong></em><br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\nAsgarath83 edited the code, and a lot of skins and some textures came from others modders. Being said, I made all the mod alone, including Mapping, Music (and not just editing them, I actually made two of them, as a musician), npcs, some gfx, voiceovers (helped by girlfriend and bestfriend), scripting, videos editing, texturing and skinning.&nbsp;<br>\nSo ECMIII took me officially one year and a half but If I count early developement (started during the finishing of ECMII), it took me almost two years.What took the most time was the Zone Of Trouble area (zone with portals), because South Plain is a central map, and I made every versions of this map and needed to compile a lot of them again and again (and this particular map was the one who takes the most time to compile...). I also needed to make every versions of the 7 levels you visit from South Plain (The Cave, Vinegar Sith HQ, North Plain, The Canyon, Glacier Cocktail, The Pyramid, The Factory), taking account of the progression of the mod, and updating Kyle capacities. End of the mod was the fastest thing to do. I took me 1 week to make the last 12 maps I think.&nbsp;<br>\nComparing to previous mods, because they are totally different mods with different goals and maps, it took me one more year. ECMI and II were basically \"killing and finding secrets\" challenges, but in ECMIII there is a little story progression, different scripts, videos and voiceovers, so the mod is a lot more complex (including new capacities, like the transforming-platforms).<br>\n<span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"https://i.imgur.com/SQ04n1o.png\"></span><br>\n<em><strong>Did the mod turn out exactly like you had initially planned it to be, or did it end up being much different?</strong></em><br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n<em><strong><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"http://i.imgur.com/cCHzEnE.png\" style=\"float: right;\"></span></strong></em><br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\nFirstly, the mod was written to revisit a lot more places from ECMI from a new point of view. It would have started in the Sand Island from ECMI (third island), have the same main villain and would have ended in this villain castle, <em>again</em>.<br>\nBut during the developpement this idea started to bore me so I only kept the Castle Ending, because Castle in ECMIII is very different from the first one (and I prefer it a lot like this).<br>\nFunny thing to notice, the mod would have been a lot shorter... Kyle was supposed to quit the Zone Of Trouble to Lawn's Land for 3 maps and enter the Castle. He was supposed to be helped by Lana and an old jedi (I used jeditrainer skin firstly) with a white lightsaber...<br>\nBut a this time, when I ended the Zone Of Trouble area, I got this special nostalgia about Toy Story 2 PC Game, when you was supposed to travel through all the city to find Woody who has been captured.&nbsp;<br>\nI took this idea, and created Duncan (the character with the white lightsaber) and decided to make 15 maps about Duncan finding a way to the castle because Kyle has been captured. But after the first one, it appears to me that 15 maps would be boring, so I just made 6 maps and decided to make the ending not only playing Kyle but also Duncan (again) and Lana (for 3 maps).&nbsp;<br>\nAnd the idea of the final map being the one you see in first when you launch the mod (the one with the cinematic) came at the very end, before making the last map.<br>\n<span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"https://i.imgur.com/SQ04n1o.png\"></span><br>\n<em><strong>Are you satisfied with the end result? What would you do to improve it?</strong></em><br>\n<em><strong><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"http://i.imgur.com/cCHzEnE.png\" style=\"float: right;\"></span></strong></em><br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\nI'm quite satisfied with the mod, because people seem to be satisfied about it. I would probably have fixed some boring bugs which would have took me hours and hours to fix (bugs in the South Plain), and I would have taken more time to do the videos and the voiceovers. And also textures. It's really not tiling in a lot of places. My girlfriend who study 3D told me it is learner's error. Such a shame, because little bugs can sometimes embarrass you more than huge plot holes.<br>\n<span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"https://i.imgur.com/SQ04n1o.png\"></span><br>\n<strong><em>Are there any projects you will be working on now that this mod is finished?</em></strong><br>\n<em><strong><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"http://i.imgur.com/cCHzEnE.png\" style=\"float: right;\"></span></strong></em><br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\nYes. I'm actually working on Epic Challenge Mod IV: Temple Of Time. The mod will be Star Wars related and will be far more realistic in some aspects. We will play a bunch of characters (including Kyle) and see different eras of SW. After ECMIV I will do a last Epic Challenge Mod, the fifth one, which will be a lot more personal. Maybe I will one day do a Hogwarts Map, when I get the mapping skill.<br>\n<span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"https://i.imgur.com/SQ04n1o.png\"></span><br>\n<strong><em>One last question. Who would win in a fight, Kyle Katarn <img src=\"https://jkhub.org/public/style_emoticons/default/kyle2.png\" class=\"bbc_emoticon\" alt=\":kyle:\"> or BB-8?&nbsp; <img src=\"https://jkhub.org/public/style_emoticons/default/bb8_2.png\" class=\"bbc_emoticon\" alt=\":bb8:\"></em></strong><br>\n<span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"http://i.imgur.com/cCHzEnE.png\" style=\"float: right;\"></span><br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\nKyle Katarn, without a doubt.<br>\n<span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"https://i.imgur.com/SQ04n1o.png\"></span></p><p><em><strong>Alright, thanks for answering my questions! Looking forward to future projects!</strong></em></p><p>&nbsp;</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p>&nbsp;</p><span style=\"font-size:24px\">In summary</span><br>\nThis is less of a review article and more of a feature, however, I do recommend playing this mod. It’s a lot of fun if you like to be challenged. There’s a lot of content to go through, a variety of enemies, challenges, and maps.<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\nThanks to RJA for taking the time to answer some questions, and good luck on future projects! You can check out one of the teasers that RJA made below, as well as the file page where you can download the mod.<br>\n&nbsp;<br>\nIf you'd like your mod to be in an article like this in the future, please PM me or another staff member, and we can work with you on that. <img src=\"https://jkhub.org/public/style_emoticons/default/smile.png\" class=\"bbc_emoticon\" alt=\":)\"><br><br><center><iframe width=\"560\" height=\"315\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/ILlgYfV4tLU?rel=0&amp;showinfo=0\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe><br>\n&nbsp;<br>\n</center><br><style>\ndiv.BBcodeButton button {\nbackground: #212121 url(https://jkhub.org/public/style_images/jkhub/topic_button.png) repeat-x <div class=\"ipsBox\">\n                        <div class=\"ipsBox_container ipsPad\">\n                                \n                                <div id=\"jkhsub\"><h2 class=\"ipsType_subtitle\">\n                                        \n\n                                        \n                                        \n                                        \n                                        <a href=\"https://jkhub.org/page/index.html/_/sitenews/happy-new-year-r135\">Happy new year!</a>\n                                </h2></div>\n                                <div class=\"desc\">Dec 31 2016 09:23 PM | <a hovercard-ref=\"member\" hovercard-id=\"1\" data-ipb=\"noparse\" class=\"url fn name  ___hover___member _hoversetup\" href=\"https://jkhub.org/user/1-caelum/\" title=\"\" id=\"anonymous_element_2\"><span itemprop=\"name\">Caelum</span></a> in <a href=\"https://jkhub.org/page/index.html/_/sitenews/\">Site news</a></div>\n                                <br>\n                                <p></p><p class=\"bbc_center\"><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"https://i.imgur.com/LfjhYsn.png\" alt=\"Posted Image\"></span></p><strong class=\"bbc\"><span style=\"font-size: 18px\">Happy new year!</span></strong><br>I promised a post with fun statistics about JKHub several months ago. First I didn't get around to doing it, and then I didn't want to steal the thunder of the Halloween and Christmas contests, but New Year's Eve seems like the perfect opportunity to post it. Before I move on to all that though: <strong class=\"bbc\">happy new year from all of us JKHub staff people</strong>!<br> <p></p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong class=\"bbc\"><span style=\"font-size: 18px\">So how many people played JKA in 2016?</span></strong><br>Honest answer: it's difficult to say. For example, about 412 players are playing as I type this according to Steam, but 123 humans are on a server according to information from the JKHub master server. It's safe to say there are at least 100 people ingame at (almost) any given time though.<br> <br>A better question to ask is: are there more players or less players? It's a better question because I can actually answer it: the number of JKA players seems to be growing slightly. Here are the number JKA players (including SP) over time according to Steam, over the past 2 years:<br> </p><p>&nbsp;</p><p></p><p class=\"bbc_center\"><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"https://i.imgur.com/1gZN1UR.png\" alt=\"Posted Image\"></span></p><p class=\"bbc_center\"><strong class=\"bbc\">Steam JKA players (incl. SP) over the past 2 years. Source: <a href=\"https://steamdb.info/app/6020/graphs/\" class=\"bbc_url\" title=\"External link\" rel=\"nofollow external\">SteamDB</a></strong></p>Can you tell when the EP7 movie was released?<p></p><p>&nbsp;</p><p>Now, the same data, over about 5 years (starting July 2012):<br> </p><p>&nbsp;</p><p></p><p class=\"bbc_center\"><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"https://i.imgur.com/6h8njHv.png\" alt=\"Posted Image\"></span></p><p class=\"bbc_center\"><strong class=\"bbc\">Steam JKA players over the past ~5 years. Source: <a href=\"http://steamcharts.com/app/6020#All\" class=\"bbc_url\" title=\"External link\" rel=\"nofollow external\">Steamcharts</a></strong></p>It's incredibly hard to see on that last chart because it's kind of horrible, but average number of ingame players steadily grows from about 150ish players (2012-2013) to over double that (2016), and while the movies clearly help, that growth is happening even if you ignore the movies.<p></p><p>&nbsp;</p><p>Now, nobody knows how that translates to Multiplayer. Steam players are just one data point, and who knows what percentage of these players are playing Multiplayer? At the very least though, it suggests JKA isn't dying as people often think: it may even be growing a bit.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong class=\"bbc\"><span style=\"font-size: 18px\">Site activity</span></strong><br>What about JKHub itself? One of the best way to measure it is number of posts. A lot of statistics are subject to bad numbers: both counting number of registrations and number of views include an unknown, but big percentage of automated bots. We're mainly interested in humans.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p>Excluding today, our forum saw a total of <strong class=\"bbc\">27346</strong> posts this year. The most active months were January (3440 posts), June (3210) and April (3050). On average, that's roughly <strong class=\"bbc\">75 posts a day</strong>. Note that a 'post' here is defined pretty broadly - I'm pretty sure our forum software counts things like status update replies and file comments as 'posts' too.<br> <br>Here's how that compares to previous years:<br><strong class=\"bbc\">2016:</strong> 27,346 posts<br><strong class=\"bbc\">2015:</strong> 22,945 posts<br><strong class=\"bbc\">2014:</strong> 10,730 posts<br> <br>For those interested, here is an obnoxiously large graph charting this out monthly over the past 4 years:<br></p><div class=\"bbc_spoiler\">\n\t<span class=\"spoiler_title\">Spoiler</span> <input type=\"button\" class=\"bbc_spoiler_show\" value=\"Show\">\n\t<div class=\"bbc_spoiler_wrapper\"><div class=\"bbc_spoiler_content\" style=\"display:none;\"><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"https://i.imgur.com/NvdSzoJ.png\" alt=\"Posted Image\"></span></div></div>\n</div><br> <br>Website activity is definitely still going up each year.<br> <br><strong class=\"bbc\"><span style=\"font-size: 18px\">Browsers &amp; OS</span></strong><br>So which browsers and operating systems do JKA players use? Again, it's difficult to measure: an unknown percentage of website views are from automated bots, headless browsers, and general non-human scum. The closest approximation I can give is by measuring the browsers &amp; operating systems used specifically to download mods though, leading to the following charts:<br> <p></p><p>&nbsp;</p><p></p><p class=\"bbc_center\"><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"https://i.imgur.com/U70cMWQ.png\" alt=\"Posted Image\"></span></p><p class=\"bbc_center\"><strong class=\"bbc\">Note:</strong> 'Mozilla' is not 'Firefox', it's an assortment of misc browsers</p> <p></p><p>&nbsp;</p><p></p><p class=\"bbc_center\"><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"https://i.imgur.com/1oJu1rP.png\" alt=\"Posted Image\"></span></p><p class=\"bbc_center\"><strong class=\"bbc\">Note:</strong> really old OSes like Windows 95 are probably spambots spoofing their user agent header rather than people actually using that OS</p><strong class=\"bbc\"><span style=\"font-size: 18px\">Recap</span></strong><br>All in all, it seems like this year has been a great year for both JKA and JKHub in terms of activity. I wish I had even more statistics to share, but unfortunately, I don't, so I'll leave it at this. Looking forward to next year, we hope to release the JKHub 2.0 redesign &amp; modernizations in 2017, and the upcoming month or two will be especially interesting to those of you who want to see more articles and news. <img src=\"https://jkhub.org/public/style_emoticons/default/smile.png\" class=\"bbc_emoticon\" alt=\":)\"><br> <br>For now, happy new year, and don't explode yourselves with fireworks. That would reflect badly on next year's activity statistics.<p></p>\n                                <br><br>\n                                <span class=\"links\">\n                                        <a href=\"https://jkhub.org/page/index.html/_/sitenews/happy-new-year-r135\" class=\"read_more\">Read story →</a>\n                                        &nbsp;&nbsp;\n                      &nbsp;&nbsp;\n                                        \n                                        \n                                </span>\n                                <br style=\"clear: both\">\n                        </div>\n                </div>\n                <br>\n        \n\n                <div class=\"ipsBox\">\n                        <div class=\"ipsBox_container ipsPad\">\n                                \n                                <div id=\"jkhsub\"><h2 class=\"ipsType_subtitle\">\n                                        \n\n                                        \n                                        \n                                        \n                                        <a href=\"https://jkhub.org/page/index.html/_/sitenews/secret-santa-2016-r134\">Secret Santa 2016</a>\n                                </h2></div>\n                                <div class=\"desc\">Nov 25 2016 11:34 PM | <a hovercard-ref=\"member\" hovercard-id=\"122\" data-ipb=\"noparse\" class=\"url fn name  ___hover___member _hoversetup\" href=\"https://jkhub.org/user/122-circa/\" title=\"\" id=\"anonymous_element_3\"><span itemprop=\"name\">Circa</span></a> in <a href=\"https://jkhub.org/page/index.html/_/sitenews/\">Site news</a></div>\n                                <br>\n                                <p></p><p class=\"bbc_center\"><span rel=\"lightbox\"><img class=\"bbc_img\" src=\"https://i.imgur.com/pCzh3md.png\" alt=\"Posted Image\"></span></p>It's that time of year again! The holidays! Every year we try to put on some kind of event related to Christmas, since that's the majority of what people celebrate around here. If you celebrate something else, you can still get into the spirit of giving by participating in this year's holiday event!<br> <br> <br><span style=\"font-size: 18px\"><strong class=\"bbc\">Secret Santa is back!</strong></span><br>We've done a Secret Santa event in the past (maybe a couple times?) and it went well, so we're trying it again this year! If you're unfamiliar with how Secret Santa works, basically you get the name of a person participating and you must create a mod or graphic of some kind for that person. They can choose to provide a list of items they want, and you can choose to make something from that list or not. Some more details below.<br> <br><span style=\"font-size: 18px\"><strong class=\"bbc\">The rules</strong></span><ul class=\"bbc\"><li>You must be a registered member.</li><li>You must be able to create a mod in JKA or JK2 of some kind or a graphic (signature, wallpaper, etc), even if it's something really simple.</li><li>You must sign up, by <a href=\"http://jkhub.org/index.php?app=members&amp;module=messaging&amp;section=send&amp;do=form&amp;fromMemberID=486\" class=\"bbc_url\" title=\"\">sending a PM to the Secret Santa account</a>, saying you're participating and/or a list of what you want.</li><li>You must have the time and motivation to complete your gift on time.</li><li>You must sign up by December 1st.</li><li>You will receive a PM from that same account containing the person and their list, on December 2nd.</li><li>You will have until December 23rd to submit your gifts to the Secret Santa account via PM, once again.</li><li>You will receive your gift on Christmas Day, December 25th.</li></ul><span style=\"font-size: 18px\"><strong class=\"bbc\">What should you ask for?</strong></span><br>It's better to make a list of simple things that people can make, not things that you've been spamming the requests forum with. If you put \"make me JK4\" or \"i just want rend2\" obviously that won't happen. Here are some examples:<ul class=\"bbc\"><li>a forum avatar or signature</li><li>a mod of Rosh saying everything backwards</li><li>a JKA-related wallpaper</li><li>a giant toothbrush saber model</li><li>a mod that replaces the chat icon with a Christmas wreath</li><li>a simple code mod</li></ul><span style=\"font-size: 18px\"><strong class=\"bbc\">What should you NOT ask for?</strong></span><ul class=\"bbc\"><li>JK4 (seriously people...)</li><li>rend2</li><li>a new playermodel of some character</li><li>a huge map (small maps might be okay, depends)</li><li>some kind of mod that involves heavy coding</li><li>a mod that makes \"Circa\" replace every mention of \"Rosh\"</li></ul>Bottom line: don't ask for something that would take months or years to make. If you don't have time to make something elaborate, your secret santa won't either.<br> <br> <br>If you fail to make your gift, you force the staff to scrounge up something last-minute, which isn't cool, so please make sure to make <em class=\"bbc\">something</em>. Also, no physical or monetary gifts or address exchanging for this. Mods and graphics only.<br> <br>And again: you can only participate if you can create a gift too. If you can't you will be denied entry into the Santa zone. <img src=\"https://jkhub.org/public/style_emoticons/default/tongue.png\" class=\"bbc_emoticon\" alt=\":P\"><br> <br>That should cover it, so if you're up for it, sign up and get your list in! <img src=\"https://jkhub.org/public/style_emoticons/default/santa.gif\" class=\"bbc_emoticon\" alt=\":santa:\"><p></p>\n
